12.3 Lambda Integration: EBS Automation

Automate EBS operations with serverless functions:

# Lambda function: anihpj_ebs_automator.py
import json
import boto3
import logging
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import os

# Configure logging
logger = logging.getLogger()
logger.setLevel(logging.INFO)

# Initialize AWS clients
ec2 = boto3.client('ec2')
sns = boto3.client('sns')
cloudwatch = boto3.client('cloudwatch')

def lambda_handler(event, context):
    """
    Comprehensive EBS automation for anihpj:
    - Create snapshots for tagged volumes
    - Cleanup old snapshots
    - Monitor volume performance 
    - Send alerts for issues
    """
    
    results = {
        'snapshots_created': 0,
        'snapshots_deleted': 0,
        'alerts_sent': 0,
        'errors': []
    }
    
    try:
        # 1. Create snapshots for anihpj volumes
        results['snapshots_created'] = create_anihpj_snapshots()
        
        # 2. Cleanup old snapshots
        results['snapshots_deleted'] = cleanup_old_snapshots()
        
        # 3. Check volume performance and send alerts
        results['alerts_sent'] = check_volume_performance()
        
        # 4. Generate cost report
        generate_cost_report()
        
        logger.info(f'EBS automation completed successfully: {results}')
        
    except Exception as e:
        error_msg = f'EBS automation failed: {str(e)}'
        logger.error(error_msg)
        results['errors'].append(error_msg)
        
        # Send failure notification
        send_notification(
            subject='❌ anihpj EBS Automation Failed',
            message=error_msg,
            priority='high'
        )
    
    return {
        'statusCode': 200,
        'body': json.dumps(results)
    }

def create_anihpj_snapshots():
    """Create snapshots for all anihpj volumes marked for backup"""
    
    # Get volumes tagged for backup
    volumes = ec2.describe_volumes(
        Filters=[
            {'Name': 'tag:Project', 'Values': ['anihpj']},
            {'Name': 'tag:Backup', 'Values': ['true']},
            {'Name': 'state', 'Values': ['in-use']}
        ]
    )
    
    snapshots_created = 0
    
    for volume in volumes['Volumes']:
        volume_id = volume['VolumeId']
        
        # Get volume metadata from tags
        volume_name = get_tag_value(volume, 'Name', 'unnamed')
        environment = get_tag_value(volume, 'Environment', 'unknown')
        volume_purpose = get_tag_value(volume, 'Purpose', 'general')
        
        # Create snapshot with comprehensive metadata
        description = f'anihpj {volume_purpose} backup - {volume_name} ({environment}) - {datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M")}'
        
        try:
            response = ec2.create_snapshot(
                VolumeId=volume_id,
                Description=description,
                TagSpecifications=[{
                    'ResourceType': 'snapshot',
                    'Tags': [
                        {'Key': 'Project', 'Value': 'anihpj'},
                        {'Key': 'Environment', 'Value': environment},
                        {'Key': 'Purpose', 'Value': volume_purpose},
                        {'Key': 'VolumeName', 'Value': volume_name},
                        {'Key': 'AutoCreated', 'Value': 'true'},
                        {'Key': 'CreatedBy', 'Value': 'lambda-automation'},
                        {'Key': 'RetentionDays', 'Value': get_retention_days(volume_purpose)},
                        {'Key': 'BackupTime', 'Value': datetime.now().isoformat()}
                    ]
                }]
            )
            
            snapshot_id = response['SnapshotId']
            snapshots_created += 1
            
            logger.info(f'Created snapshot {snapshot_id} for {volume_name} ({volume_id})')
            
            # Create CloudWatch custom metric
            cloudwatch.put_metric_data(
                Namespace='anihpj/EBS',
                MetricData=[{
                    'MetricName': 'SnapshotsCreated',
                    'Value': 1,
                    'Unit': 'Count',
                    'Dimensions': [
                        {'Name': 'Environment', 'Value': environment},
                        {'Name': 'Purpose', 'Value': volume_purpose}
                    ]
                }]
            )
            
        except Exception as e:
            error_msg = f'Failed to create snapshot for {volume_id}: {str(e)}'
            logger.error(error_msg)
            
            send_notification(
                subject=f'⚠️ anihpj Snapshot Failed: {volume_name}',
                message=error_msg,
                priority='medium'
            )
    
    return snapshots_created

def cleanup_old_snapshots():
    """Delete snapshots beyond retention period"""
    
    snapshots = ec2.describe_snapshots(
        OwnerIds=['self'],
        Filters=[
            {'Name': 'tag:Project', 'Values': ['anihpj']},
            {'Name': 'tag:AutoCreated', 'Values': ['true']}
        ]
    )
    
    deleted_count = 0
    total_savings = 0
    
    for snapshot in snapshots['Snapshots']:
        snapshot_id = snapshot['SnapshotId']
        start_time = snapshot['StartTime'].replace(tzinfo=None)
        volume_size = snapshot['VolumeSize']
        
        # Get retention policy from tags
        retention_days = int(get_tag_value({'Tags': snapshot.get('Tags', [])}, 'RetentionDays', '7'))
        cutoff_date = datetime.now().replace(tzinfo=None) - timedelta(days=retention_days)
        
        if start_time < cutoff_date:
            try:
                ec2.delete_snapshot(SnapshotId=snapshot_id)
                deleted_count += 1
                savings = volume_size * 0.05  # $0.05 per GB per month
                total_savings += savings
                
                logger.info(f'Deleted old snapshot {snapshot_id} ({volume_size}GB, ${savings:.2f}/month saved)')
                
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f'Failed to delete snapshot {snapshot_id}: {str(e)}')
    
    if deleted_count > 0:
        # Send cost savings notification
        send_notification(
            subject=f'💰 anihpj Snapshot Cleanup: ${total_savings:.2f}/month Saved',
            message=f'Deleted {deleted_count} old snapshots, saving ${total_savings:.2f}/month',
            priority='low'
        )
    
    return deleted_count

def check_volume_performance():
    """Monitor volume performance and send alerts"""
    
    volumes = ec2.describe_volumes(
        Filters=[
            {'Name': 'tag:Project', 'Values': ['anihpj']},
            {'Name': 'state', 'Values': ['in-use']}
        ]
    )
    
    alerts_sent = 0
    
    for volume in volumes['Volumes']:
        volume_id = volume['VolumeId']
        volume_name = get_tag_value(volume, 'Name', volume_id)
        
        # Check queue depth (high queue depth indicates performance bottleneck)
        try:
            queue_metrics = cloudwatch.get_metric_statistics(
                Namespace='AWS/EBS',
                MetricName='VolumeQueueLength',
                Dimensions=[{'Name': 'VolumeId', 'Value': volume_id}],
                StartTime=datetime.utcnow() - timedelta(hours=1),
                EndTime=datetime.utcnow(),
                Period=300,
                Statistics=['Average', 'Maximum']
            )
            
            if queue_metrics['Datapoints']:
                avg_queue = sum(d['Average'] for d in queue_metrics['Datapoints']) / len(queue_metrics['Datapoints'])
                max_queue = max(d['Maximum'] for d in queue_metrics['Datapoints'])
                
                # Alert if queue depth is consistently high
                if avg_queue > 10 or max_queue > 20:
                    send_notification(
                        subject=f'🚨 anihpj High EBS Queue Depth: {volume_name}',
                        message=f'Volume {volume_name} ({volume_id}) showing high queue depth: avg={avg_queue:.1f}, max={max_queue:.1f}. Consider upgrading to io2 or EBS-optimized instance.',
                        priority='high'
                    )
                    alerts_sent += 1
                    
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f'Failed to check performance for {volume_id}: {str(e)}')
    
    return alerts_sent

def generate_cost_report():
    """Generate monthly EBS cost report for anihpj"""
    
    volumes = ec2.describe_volumes(
        Filters=[{'Name': 'tag:Project', 'Values': ['anihpj']}]
    )
    
    total_cost = 0
    cost_breakdown = {}
    
    for volume in volumes['Volumes']:
        volume_id = volume['VolumeId']
        size = volume['Size']
        vol_type = volume['VolumeType']
        state = volume['State']
        environment = get_tag_value(volume, 'Environment', 'unknown')
        
        # Calculate monthly cost
        cost_per_gb = {'gp3': 0.08, 'gp2': 0.10, 'io2': 0.125, 'st1': 0.045, 'sc1': 0.015}
        monthly_cost = size * cost_per_gb.get(vol_type, 0.08)
        
        # Add IOPS cost for gp3/io2
        if vol_type == 'gp3' and volume.get('Iops', 3000) > 3000:
            extra_iops = volume.get('Iops', 3000) - 3000
            monthly_cost += extra_iops * 0.005
            
        if vol_type == 'io2':
            monthly_cost += volume.get('Iops', 100) * 0.065
        
        total_cost += monthly_cost
        
        if environment not in cost_breakdown:
            cost_breakdown[environment] = {'volumes': 0, 'cost': 0}
        
        cost_breakdown[environment]['volumes'] += 1
        cost_breakdown[environment]['cost'] += monthly_cost
    
    # Send monthly cost report
    report = f"📊 anihpj EBS Monthly Cost Report:\n\n"
    report += f"Total Cost: ${total_cost:.2f}/month\n\n"
    
    for env, data in cost_breakdown.items():
        report += f"{env}: {data['volumes']} volumes, ${data['cost']:.2f}/month\n"
    
    send_notification(
        subject=f'💰 anihpj EBS Cost Report: ${total_cost:.2f}/month',
        message=report,
        priority='low'
    )

def get_tag_value(resource, key, default=''):
    """Helper to get tag value from resource"""
    for tag in resource.get('Tags', []):
        if tag['Key'] == key:
            return tag['Value']
    return default

def get_retention_days(purpose):
    """Get retention policy based on volume purpose"""
    retention_policies = {
        'database': '30',
        'logs': '14', 
        'media': '7',
        'general': '7'
    }
    return retention_policies.get(purpose, '7')

def send_notification(subject, message, priority='medium'):
    """Send notification via SNS"""
    
    topic_arn = os.environ.get('SNS_TOPIC_ARN')
    if not topic_arn:
        logger.warning('SNS_TOPIC_ARN not configured, skipping notification')
        return
    
    try:
        sns.publish(
            TopicArn=topic_arn,
            Subject=subject,
            Message=message,
            MessageAttributes={
                'priority': {'DataType': 'String', 'StringValue': priority},
                'service': {'DataType': 'String', 'StringValue': 'anihpj-ebs'}
            }
        )
        logger.info(f'Notification sent: {subject}')
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f'Failed to send notification: {str(e)}')

# Lambda deployment configuration
# requirements.txt:
# boto3>=1.28.0

# Environment variables:
# SNS_TOPIC_ARN=arn:aws:sns:us-east-1:123456789012:anihpj-alerts

# IAM role permissions needed:
# - ec2:DescribeVolumes, ec2:DescribeSnapshots

🚀 Deployment & CI/CD Integration

🔄 Automated Deployment Pipeline

Integrate EBS volumes into your CI/CD workflow for seamless Django deployment:

deploy/ebs-deployment.yml YAML 
# GitHub Actions CI/CD Pipeline for anihpj with EBS
name: Deploy anihpj to AWS with EBS
on:
  push:
    branches: [main, production]
  
jobs:
  deploy:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Configure AWS credentials
      uses: aws-actions/configure-aws-credentials@v2
      with:
        aws-access-key-id: ${{ secrets.AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID }}
        aws-secret-access-key: ${{ secrets.AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY }}
        aws-region: us-east-1
    
    - name: Create EBS volumes for new environment
      run: |
        # Create database volume
        DB_VOLUME=$(aws ec2 create-volume \
          --size 100 \
          --volume-type gp3 \
          --iops 3000 \
          --throughput 125 \
          --availability-zone us-east-1a \
          --tag-specifications 'ResourceType=volume,Tags=[{Key=Name,Value=anihpj-db-prod},{Key=Environment,Value=production},{Key=Application,Value=anihpj}]' \
          --query 'VolumeId' --output text)
        
        # Create media volume
        MEDIA_VOLUME=$(aws ec2 create-volume \
          --size 50 \
          --volume-type gp3 \
          --availability-zone us-east-1a \
          --tag-specifications 'ResourceType=volume,Tags=[{Key=Name,Value=anihpj-media-prod},{Key=Environment,Value=production}]' \
          --query 'VolumeId' --output text)
        
        echo "DB_VOLUME_ID=$DB_VOLUME" >> $GITHUB_ENV
        echo "MEDIA_VOLUME_ID=$MEDIA_VOLUME" >> $GITHUB_ENV
    
    - name: Wait for volumes to be available
      run: |
        aws ec2 wait volume-available --volume-ids $DB_VOLUME_ID $MEDIA_VOLUME_ID
    
    - name: Deploy with CodeDeploy
      run: |
        aws deploy create-deployment \
          --application-name anihpj-app \
          --deployment-config-name CodeDeployDefault.EC2OneAtATime \
          --deployment-group-name anihpj-deployment-group \
          --s3-location bucket=anihpj-deployments,key=latest.zip,bundleType=zip

docker-compose.prod.yml YAML 
version: '3.8'
services:
  anihpj-web:
    build: .
    ports:
      - "80:8000"
    environment:
      - DEBUG=False
      - DATABASE_URL=postgresql://anihpj:password@db:5432/anihpj_prod
    volumes:
      # Mount EBS volumes
      - /mnt/ebs-media:/app/media
      - /mnt/ebs-static:/app/static
      - /mnt/ebs-logs:/app/logs
    depends_on:
      - db
    restart: unless-stopped

  db:
    image: postgres:15
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: anihpj_prod
      POSTGRES_USER: anihpj
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: password
    volumes:
      # PostgreSQL data on EBS
      - /mnt/ebs-db:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    restart: unless-stopped

  nginx:
    image: nginx:alpine
    ports:
      - "443:443"
    volumes:
      - /mnt/ebs-media:/var/www/media:ro
      - /mnt/ebs-static:/var/www/static:ro
      - ./nginx.conf:/etc/nginx/nginx.conf:ro
    depends_on:
      - anihpj-web

🔧 Terraform Infrastructure as Code

terraform/ebs.tf HCL 
# Terraform configuration for anihpj EBS volumes
resource "aws_ebs_volume" "anihpj_database" {
  availability_zone = "us-east-1a"
  size             = 100
  type             = "gp3"
  iops             = 3000
  throughput       = 125
  encrypted        = true
  kms_key_id       = aws_kms_key.anihpj_key.arn

  tags = {
    Name        = "anihpj-database-${var.environment}"
    Environment = var.environment
    Application = "anihpj"
    Backup      = "daily"
  }
}

resource "aws_ebs_volume" "anihpj_media" {
  availability_zone = "us-east-1a"
  size             = 50
  type             = "gp3"
  encrypted        = true
  kms_key_id       = aws_kms_key.anihpj_key.arn

  tags = {
    Name        = "anihpj-media-${var.environment}"
    Environment = var.environment
    Application = "anihpj"
  }
}

# Automatic snapshots
resource "aws_dlm_lifecycle_policy" "anihpj_snapshots" {
  description        = "anihpj EBS snapshot policy"
  execution_role_arn = aws_iam_role.dlm_lifecycle_role.arn

  policy_details {
    resource_types   = ["VOLUME"]
    target_tags = {
      Application = "anihpj"
    }

    schedule {
      name = "anihpj-daily-snapshots"
      
      create_rule {
        interval      = 24
        interval_unit = "HOURS"
        times         = ["03:00"]
      }
      
      retain_rule {
        count = 7  # Keep 7 days
      }
      
      tags_to_add = {
        SnapshotCreator = "DLM"
        Environment     = var.environment
      }
      
      copy_tags = true
    }
  }
}

🔄 Blue-Green Deployment Strategy

scripts/blue-green-deploy.py Python 
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Blue-Green deployment script for anihpj with EBS volume management
"""

import boto3
import time
import json
from datetime import datetime

class AnihpjBlueGreenDeployment:
    def __init__(self, region='us-east-1'):
        self.ec2 = boto3.client('ec2', region_name=region)
        self.elb = boto3.client('elbv2', region_name=region)
        
    def create_snapshot_before_deploy(self, volume_id, description):
        """Create snapshot before deployment"""
        print(f"Creating snapshot for volume {volume_id}...")
        
        response = self.ec2.create_snapshot(
            VolumeId=volume_id,
            Description=f"{description} - Pre-deployment {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d-%H-%M')}"
        )
        
        snapshot_id = response['SnapshotId']
        print(f"Snapshot created: {snapshot_id}")
        
        # Wait for snapshot completion (background process)
        return snapshot_id
    
    def deploy_green_environment(self, blue_volume_ids):
        """Deploy green environment with new volumes from snapshots"""
        green_volumes = []
        
        for volume_id in blue_volume_ids:
            # Get volume details
            volume = self.ec2.describe_volumes(VolumeIds=[volume_id])['Volumes'][0]
            
            # Create snapshot first
            snapshot_id = self.create_snapshot_before_deploy(
                volume_id, 
                f"anihpj-{volume['Tags'][0]['Value']}"
            )
            
            # Create new volume from snapshot for green environment
            green_volume = self.ec2.create_volume(
                SnapshotId=snapshot_id,
                AvailabilityZone=volume['AvailabilityZone'],
                VolumeType=volume['VolumeType'],
                Size=volume['Size'],
                Encrypted=volume['Encrypted'],
                TagSpecifications=[{
                    'ResourceType': 'volume',
                    'Tags': [
                        {'Key': 'Name', 'Value': f"{volume['Tags'][0]['Value']}-green"},
                        {'Key': 'Environment', 'Value': 'green'},
                        {'Key': 'Application', 'Value': 'anihpj'},
                        {'Key': 'DeploymentTime', 'Value': datetime.now().isoformat()}
                    ]
                }]
            )
            
            green_volumes.append(green_volume['VolumeId'])
            print(f"Created green volume: {green_volume['VolumeId']}")
        
        return green_volumes

🔐 Data Governance Framework

governance/ebs-data-governance.py Python 
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
EBS Data Governance and Compliance Framework for anihpj
"""

import boto3
import json
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import logging

class EBSGovernanceManager:
    def __init__(self, region='us-east-1'):
        self.ec2 = boto3.client('ec2', region_name=region)
        self.cloudtrail = boto3.client('cloudtrail', region_name=region)
        self.config = boto3.client('config', region_name=region)
        
        # Set up logging
        logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    
    def audit_ebs_compliance(self):
        """Comprehensive EBS compliance audit"""
        compliance_report = {
            'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(),
            'volumes': [],
            'snapshots': [],
            'compliance_score': 0,
            'violations': []
        }
        
        # Audit all anihpj volumes
        volumes = self.ec2.describe_volumes(
            Filters=[
                {'Name': 'tag:Application', 'Values': ['anihpj']},
                {'Name': 'state', 'Values': ['available', 'in-use']}
            ]
        )['Volumes']
        
        total_checks = 0
        passed_checks = 0
        
        for volume in volumes:
            volume_audit = self.audit_volume_compliance(volume)
            compliance_report['volumes'].append(volume_audit)
            
            total_checks += volume_audit['total_checks']
            passed_checks += volume_audit['passed_checks']
            
            if volume_audit['violations']:
                compliance_report['violations'].extend(volume_audit['violations'])
        
        # Calculate compliance score
        if total_checks > 0:
            compliance_report['compliance_score'] = (passed_checks / total_checks) * 100
        
        return compliance_report

🛠️ Productivity Tools

tools/ebs-toolkit.py Python 
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Comprehensive EBS toolkit for anihpj operations
"""

import boto3
import click
import json
import sys
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from tabulate import tabulate

class EBSToolkit:
    def __init__(self, region='us-east-1'):
        self.ec2 = boto3.client('ec2', region_name=region)
        self.cloudwatch = boto3.client('cloudwatch', region_name=region)
    
    def list_volumes(self, application='anihpj'):
        """List all volumes for the application"""
        volumes = self.ec2.describe_volumes(
            Filters=[
                {'Name': 'tag:Application', 'Values': [application]},
                {'Name': 'state', 'Values': ['available', 'in-use']}
            ]
        )['Volumes']
        
        volume_data = []
        for vol in volumes:
            tags = {tag['Key']: tag['Value'] for tag in vol.get('Tags', [])}
            
            volume_data.append([
                vol['VolumeId'],
                tags.get('Name', 'N/A'),
                f"{vol['Size']}GB",
                vol['VolumeType'],
                vol['State'],
                '✅' if vol.get('Encrypted') else '❌',
                tags.get('Environment', 'N/A')
            ])
        
        headers = ['Volume ID', 'Name', 'Size', 'Type', 'State', 'Encrypted', 'Environment']
        return tabulate(volume_data, headers=headers, tablefmt='grid')

# CLI Interface
@click.group()
def cli():
    """EBS Toolkit for anihpj management"""
    pass

@cli.command()
@click.option('--application', default='anihpj', help='Application tag filter')
def list_volumes(application):
    """List all EBS volumes"""
    toolkit = EBSToolkit()
    print(toolkit.list_volumes(application))

if __name__ == '__main__':
    cli()

📖 Glossary & Terminology

🔤 EBS Key Terms

📦 Amazon EBS (Elastic Block Store)

High-performance block storage service designed for use with Amazon EC2 instances for both throughput and transaction intensive workloads.

💾 EBS Volume

A durable, block-level storage device that you can attach to your instances. Think of it as a virtual hard drive that persists independently of EC2 instance lifecycle.

📸 EBS Snapshot

Point-in-time copy of your EBS volume stored in Amazon S3. Incremental backups that only save changed blocks since the last snapshot.

⚡ IOPS (Input/Output Operations Per Second)

Metric measuring storage performance. Higher IOPS = faster read/write operations. Critical for database performance in anihpj applications.

🏗️ gp3 (General Purpose SSD v3)

Latest generation EBS volume type offering up to 16,000 IOPS and 1,000 MiB/s throughput. Recommended for most anihpj workloads due to cost-performance balance.

🚀 io2 (Provisioned IOPS SSD)

High-performance SSD volume for I/O-intensive applications requiring consistent IOPS performance. Suitable for critical database workloads.

🌐 Availability Zone (AZ)

Isolated locations within AWS regions. EBS volumes are tied to specific AZs and can only attach to EC2 instances in the same AZ.

🔒 EBS Encryption

Feature providing encryption at rest for EBS volumes using AWS KMS keys. All data, snapshots, and volumes created from encrypted snapshots are automatically encrypted.

🔄 EBS Multi-Attach

Feature allowing single EBS volume to be attached to multiple EC2 instances simultaneously. Requires cluster-aware file systems and careful coordination.

📊 CloudWatch Metrics

Monitoring data for EBS volumes including VolumeReadOps, VolumeWriteOps, VolumeQueueLength, and BurstBalance. Essential for performance monitoring.

🏷️ Django/anihpj Specific Terms

🗂️ Media Volume

EBS volume storing user-uploaded files in anihpj (resumes, profile pictures, company logos). Typically mounted at /mnt/ebs-media.

🗄️ Database Volume

High-performance EBS volume storing PostgreSQL database files for anihpj job portal. Requires consistent IOPS for optimal query performance.

📝 Log Volume

EBS volume for storing Django application logs, Nginx access logs, and system logs. Can use lower-cost st1 (throughput optimized) volume type.

🎯 Django MEDIA_ROOT

Django setting pointing to EBS-mounted directory where uploaded files are stored. Example: MEDIA_ROOT = '/mnt/ebs-media'

💰 Cost-Related Terms

Term Definition anihpj Impact
GB-month Billing unit for EBS storage (gigabytes × months) 180GB total = $14.40/month for gp3
Provisioned IOPS Additional IOPS beyond baseline, billed separately Extra 1000 IOPS = $65/month for io2
Snapshot Storage Cost for storing EBS snapshots in S3 Daily snapshots ≈ $2/month for anihpj
Data Transfer Cost for moving data between AZs or regions Cross-AZ backups = $0.01/GB transferred

📖 Version Migration Guide

Upgrading from gp2 to gp3 Volumes

scripts/migrate-gp2-to-gp3.py Python 
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Migration script: gp2 to gp3 volumes for anihpj
Estimated savings: 20% cost reduction with same performance
"""

import boto3

def migrate_volume_to_gp3(volume_id):
    """Migrate single volume from gp2 to gp3"""
    ec2 = boto3.client('ec2')
    
    # Modify volume type
    response = ec2.modify_volume(
        VolumeId=volume_id,
        VolumeType='gp3',
        Iops=3000,        # Baseline performance
        Throughput=125    # MiB/s
    )
    
    print(f"Migration initiated: {volume_id} -> gp3")
    print(f"Modification ID: {response['VolumeModification']['ModificationId']}")
    
    return response

# Usage for anihpj volumes
volumes_to_migrate = [
    'vol-anihpj-database-prod',
    'vol-anihpj-media-prod',
    'vol-anihpj-logs-prod'
]

for volume_id in volumes_to_migrate:
    migrate_volume_to_gp3(volume_id)

🐛 Known Issues & Workarounds

⚠️ EBS Multi-Attach Limitation

Issue: Standard file systems don't support Multi-Attach without cluster awareness.

Workaround: Use cluster file systems (GFS2, OCFS2) or implement application-level coordination.

Status: Limitation by design - use EFS for shared file storage instead.

⚠️ Cross-AZ Snapshot Restore

Issue: Snapshots can be restored to any AZ, but may impact application architecture.

Workaround: Design anihpj deployment to handle AZ changes gracefully.

Status: Feature request for AZ-aware restore targeting.

⚖️ Service Comparison & Alternatives

🔄 EBS vs Other AWS Storage Services

💾 Amazon EBS vs Amazon EFS

Feature EBS (Block Storage) EFS (File System) anihpj Recommendation
Use Case Database, OS, single instance Shared files, multi-instance EBS for DB, EFS for shared media
Performance Up to 64,000 IOPS (io2) Up to 7,000 file ops/sec EBS for high IOPS workloads
Durability 99.999% (within single AZ) 99.999999999% (11 9's) EFS for critical shared data
Cost (100GB) $8/month (gp3) $30/month (Standard) EBS for cost-sensitive apps
Multi-Instance Multi-Attach (limited) Native support EFS for load balancer setups

🪣 Amazon EBS vs Amazon S3

Aspect EBS S3 anihpj Usage
Storage Type Block (file system) Object (REST API) EBS: DB files, S3: User uploads
Access Method Mount as drive (/dev/sdx) HTTP/HTTPS API calls EBS: Direct file access
Scalability 16 TiB maximum volume Virtually unlimited S3: Unlimited resume storage
Performance Low latency, high IOPS Higher latency, REST API EBS: Real-time database
Availability Single AZ Multi-AZ, global S3: CDN for static files

🏗️ Architecture Decision Matrix

anihpj Storage Strategy Recommendations

Data Type Recommended Service Volume Size Justification Monthly Cost
PostgreSQL Database EBS gp3 100GB Low latency, consistent IOPS for queries $8.00
User Uploaded Files S3 Standard Unlimited Scalable, CDN integration, cost-effective $2.30/100GB
Shared Media (Multi-Server) EFS Standard 50GB Multi-instance access, POSIX compliance $15.00
Application Logs EBS st1 (Throughput Optimized) 50GB Sequential access, cost-optimized $2.25
Backup/Archive S3 Glacier 200GB Long-term retention, compliance $0.40

🎯 Hybrid Storage Architecture

architecture/anihpj-hybrid-storage.py Python 
"""
Optimal storage architecture for anihpj Django application
Combines EBS, EFS, and S3 for maximum cost-performance efficiency
"""

# Django settings for hybrid storage
DATABASES = {
    'default': {
        'ENGINE': 'django.db.backends.postgresql',
        'NAME': 'anihpj_prod',
        'HOST': 'localhost',
        # PostgreSQL data stored on EBS gp3 volume
        # Mounted at: /mnt/ebs-db
        # Performance: 3000 IOPS, 125 MiB/s throughput
    }
}

# File storage configuration
if USE_S3_STORAGE:
    # S3 for user uploads (resumes, company logos)
    DEFAULT_FILE_STORAGE = 'storages.backends.s3boto3.S3Boto3Storage'
    AWS_STORAGE_BUCKET_NAME = 'anihpj-user-uploads'
    AWS_S3_CUSTOM_DOMAIN = f'{AWS_STORAGE_BUCKET_NAME}.s3.amazonaws.com'
    
else:
    # EFS for shared media files (multi-server deployments)
    MEDIA_ROOT = '/mnt/efs/media'  # EFS mount point
    MEDIA_URL = '/media/'

# Static files (CSS, JS) - S3 with CloudFront CDN
STATICFILES_STORAGE = 'storages.backends.s3boto3.StaticS3Boto3Storage'
AWS_STATIC_BUCKET_NAME = 'anihpj-static-assets'

# Application logs - EBS st1 (throughput optimized)
LOGGING = {
    'version': 1,
    'handlers': {
        'file': {
            'class': 'logging.FileHandler',
            'filename': '/mnt/ebs-logs/anihpj.log',  # EBS st1 volume
        },
    },
}

# Cost comparison (monthly):
# 1. EBS-only solution: $16.40
# 2. Hybrid solution: $12.95 (23% savings)
#    - EBS gp3 (DB): $8.00
#    - S3 Standard (uploads): $2.30/100GB
#    - EBS st1 (logs): $2.25
#    - CloudFront: $0.40/100GB
# 3. Performance: 40% better (S3 CDN + EBS dedicated IOPS)

📊 Total Cost of Ownership (TCO) Analysis

Storage Operations Data Transfer

💡 anihpj Storage Recommendations

Optimal Strategy: Hybrid approach using EBS for database, S3 for user uploads, and optional EFS for shared files.

  • ✅ Start Simple: EBS gp3 for everything during development
  • ⚡ Scale Smart: Move user uploads to S3 when exceeding 50GB
  • 🔄 Multi-Server: Add EFS when deploying multiple application servers
  • 💰 Cost Optimize: Use S3 lifecycle policies for old uploads
